The store will not work correctly when cookies are disabled.

VIQRC Mix & Match Game Manual

**# Changelog**

Version 3.0 - January 29, 2026

- Expanded <G4d> to clarify that unmodified Hero Bots are always legal for use
- Added a new clause to [<SC1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc1) to specify that scores shouldn’t be adjusted for [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) in most cases
- Revised [<SC3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc3) to allow a nested [Stack](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) that is supported by any part of the [Standoff Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#standoffgoal) to count as roughly vertical
- Updated <SC5ci> to include only [Stacks](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) that are touching the PET sheet
- Updated [<T6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t6) and [<T7>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t7) to allow the use of double-sided tape to hold down [Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal) templates, and to specify that the field reset markers are not required
- Updated [<T15>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t15) to clarify the number of skills attempts available to each [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) at a league session
- Added significant Q&A boxes throughout the manual
- Minor typo / formatting fixes

Version 2.2 - December 4, 2025

- Updated Figures V-1 and V-3 to clarify intent
- Added new clauses to [<SC3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc3) to clarify “roughly vertical”
- Updated <SE3> and <SE9> to reflect the updated guidelines for “roughly vertical”
- Expanded the blue box of [<G4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g4) to clarify rule enforcement
- Updated [<G5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g5) to clarify “ [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers)”, rather than “Drivers”
- Added a new bullet to [<GG1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg1) to clarify that anyone who is not a [Drive Team Member](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) cannot coach or affect the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match)
- Updated [<GG10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg10) and [<RSC5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc5) to clarify intent regarding a [Drive Team Member](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) resetting a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) and [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject)
- Updated bullets in <SG1c> to indicate which teams are red and blue in VEXvia
- Added a bullet to [<R3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r3) to specify that event staff are allowed to take pictures of [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) as needed
- Added a bullet to <RSC7> to clarify that [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) cannot use [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) controllers for any purpose during [Autonomous Coding Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch)
- Revised [<T5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t5) to include [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) positions, and specified that [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) rotation doesn’t matter
- Added significant Q&A boxes throughout the manual
- Minor typo / formatting fixes

Version 2.1 - October 9, 2025

- Updated Figure FO-2 to show correct [Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal) boundaries
- Updated the definition of [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) to provide clarity
- Updated the definition of [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) to clarify that [Minor Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation) carry over into [Finals Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch), unless otherwise specified
- Added [CoC-related Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) as a defined term
- Added additional flowcharts under the definition of [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) to provide guidance
- Added a bullet to [<G1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g1), stating that event attendees are not allowed to record audio or video of [Teams'](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) discussions with [Head Referees](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) or other event staff/volunteers
- Split [<G4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g4) into two rules and rewrote it, to clarify intent
- Added rule [<G5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g5)
- Updated <GG2a> to clarify that [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) that participate in zero [Qualification Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#qualificationmatch) cannot be considered for judged awards
- Updated <SG5b> to clarify intent
- Revise the definition of [Practice Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#practicematch) to specify that most [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) from [Practice Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#practicematch) aren’t recorded
- Updated [<T7>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t7) to clarify that all Robot Skills Challenge Fields must be consistent with each other
- Revised <T15a> to clarify intent
- Added significant Q&A boxes throughout the manual
- Minor typo / formatting fixes

Version 2.0 - September 4, 2025

- Revised [<GG1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg1) to clarify that only three [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) can attend a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match)
- Revised [<GG2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg2) to clarify that the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) must remain at the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) for the entire duration of the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match)
- Revised [<GG4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg4) and added a blue box to remove penalties for reaching over the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) in ways that are safe and don’t impact the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match)
- Updated [<R13>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r13) to clarify that 3D printed parts are allowed for controller attachments
- Updated <RSC5aii> to clarify intent
- Added significant Q&A boxes throughout the manual
- Minor typo / formatting fixes

Version 1.1 - August 7, 2025

- Updated figure FO-2 to show the correct [Floor Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floorgoal) outline
- Added a new figure to [<SC3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc3) to show examples of nested [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin)
- Revised and expanded [<SC5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc5) to clarify how [Stacks](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) can qualify as [Placed](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#placed) in the [Standoff Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#standoffgoal)
- Updated [<SG4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg4) to clarify that a neutral object that leaves the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) must be given to the Loader in the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) closest to where it left the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), and added a Violation Note
- Updated [<SG6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg6) and added new bullet points to revise [Loading](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#load) criteria
- Updated [<RSC3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc3) and added bullet points to clarify the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) and [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) setup
- Added significant Q&A boxes throughout the manual
- Minor typo / formatting fixes

Version 1.0 - June 26, 2025

- Revised the definition of [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) to differentiate between intentional actions and intentional [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation)
- Added a note to [<SC3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc3) to clarify the definition of “fully nested”
- Revised [<SC6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc6) to clarify cases where [Stacks](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) are [Connected](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#connected) to [Beams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#beam)
- Updated <SG1d> to clarify intent
- Updated <SG4c> to clarify intent
- Revised [<RSC3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc3) to clarify how [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) can be [Loaded](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#load) in [Robot Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch)
- Updated <T1e> to clarify that [Head Referees](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) must follow the rules in the game manual
- Added significant Q&A boxes throughout the manual

Version 0.2 - June 5, 2025

- Added a link to the obsoleted game manual version in the “Updates” section, to use as a reference during update grace periods
- Clarified that the most current version of the English language PDF of the manual (this document) takes precedence over any other supplemental or translated material
- Revised [<SC1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc1) to clarify intent regarding driving after the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) timer ends
- Updated <GG1a> to clarify that devices are allowed in the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation), but may not be used for any reason during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). Using devices for translation purposes post- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) is allowed
- Expanded [<GG12>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg12) to include starting the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) before the timer begins
- Clarified that vertical expansion is unlimited in [<SG3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg3)
- Updated <SG6a> to clarify intent for where [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) may be introduced
- Added <RSC4d> to clarify intent
- Other minor typo & formatting fixes

Version 0.1 - May 14, 2025

- Initial Release

**# Quick Reference Guide**

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Scoring Rules |
| [<SC1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc1) | All scoring statuses are evaluated after the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) ends |
| [<SC2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc2) | All scoring statuses are evaluated visually by a [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) |
| [<SC3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc3) | A [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) can be [Connected](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#connected) to another [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) to form a [Stack](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) |
| [<SC4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc4) | A [Stack](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) that includes more than one color of [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) receives additional points |
| [<SC5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc5) | A [Stack](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) is considered [Placed](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#placed) in a [Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal) if it meets all of the following criteria |
| [<SC6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc6) | [Matching Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#matchinggoal) bonus criteria |
| [<SC7>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc7) | [Cleared](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#cleared) [Starting Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#startingpin) criteria |
| [<SC8>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc7) | Ending the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) in contact with [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) |

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Safety Rules |
| [<S1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#s1) | Stay safe, don’t damage the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) |
| [<S2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#s2) | [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) must be accompanied by an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) |
| [<S3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#s3) | Each [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) member must have a completed participant release form on file |

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| General Rules |
| [<G1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g1) | Treat everyone with respect |
| [<G2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g2) | VIQRC is a [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student)-centered program |
| [<G3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g3) | Use common sense |
| [<G4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g4) | All work must represent the skill level of the [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) on the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team). |
| [<G5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g5) | Each [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) can only belong to one [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team). |

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| General Game Rules |
| [<GG1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg1) | [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) drive your [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), and stay in the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) |
| [<GG2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg2) | A [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) should attend every [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) |
| [<GG3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg3) | [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) on the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) must be ready to play |
| [<GG4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg4) | Hands out of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) |
| [<GG5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg5) | [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) Replays are allowed, but rare |
| [<GG6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg6) | [Disqualifications](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification) |
| [<GG7>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg7) | Timeouts |
| [<GG8>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg8) | Keep your [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) together |
| [<GG9>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg9) | Don’t damage the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) |
| [<GG10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg10) | Handling the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) mid- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) is allowed under certain circumstances |
| [<GG11>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg11) | A [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) two [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) switch Controllers midway through the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) |
| [<GG12>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg12) | Don’t Start Before the Timer, and Stop Moving at the end of the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) |
| [<GG13>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg13) | Ending a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) early |

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Specific Game Rules |
| [<SG1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg1) | Starting a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) |
| [<SG2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg2) | Horizontal expansion is limited |
| [<SG3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg3) | Vertical expansion is unlimited |
| [<SG4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg4) | Keep [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) in the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) |
| [<SG5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg5) | Each [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) gets one Pin as a [Preload](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#preload) |
| [<SG6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg6) | Using the [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone) |

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Robot Rules |
| [<R1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r1) | One [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) per [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) |
| [<R2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r2) | [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) must represent the [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) skill level |
| [<R3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r3) | [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) must pass inspection |
| [<R4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r4) | There is a difference between accidentally and willfully violating a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) rule |
| [<R5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r5) | [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) must fit within an 11” x 20” x 15” (279.4mm x 508mm x 381.0mm) volume |
| [<R6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r6) | Officially registered [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) numbers must be displayed on [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) [License Plates](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#licenseplate) |
| [<R7>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r7) | Let it go after the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) is over |
| [<R8>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r8) | [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) have one Brain |
| [<R9>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r9) | Keep the power button accessible |
| [<R10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r10) | Firmware |
| [<R11>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r11) | Motors |
| [<R12>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r12) | Batteries |
| [<R13>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r13) | One Controller per [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) |
| [<R14>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r14) | [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) are built from the VEX IQ product line |
| [<R15>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r15) | Prohibited items |
| [<R16>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r16) | Legal Non-VEX IQ components |
| [<R17>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r17) | Decorations are allowed |
| [<R18>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r18) | Pneumatics |
| [<R19>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r19) | Modifications of parts |

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Robot Skills Challenge Rules |
| [<RSC1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc1) | Standard rules apply in most cases |
| [<RSC2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc2) | Scoring [Robot Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch) |
| [<RSC3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc3) | [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) and [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) setup for [Robot Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch) |
| [<RSC4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc4) | Loader and [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) differences |
| [<RSC5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc5) | Handling [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) during an [Autonomous Coding Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch) |
| [<RSC6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc6) | Starting an [Autonomous Coding Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch) |
| [<RSC7>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc7) | Autonomous means “no humans” |
| [<RSC8>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc8) | [Skills Stop Time](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#skillsstoptime) |

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Tournament Rules |
| [<T1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t1) | The [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) has final authority on all gameplay and [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) ruling decisions |
| [<T2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t2) | [Head Referees](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) must be qualified |
| [<T3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t3) | [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) are permitted to immediately appeal the [Head Referee’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) ruling |
| [<T4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t4) | The [Event Partner](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) have final authority regarding all non-gameplay decisions |
| [<T5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t5) | Be prepared for minor [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) variance |
| [<T6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t6) | [Fields](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) and Field Elements may be repaired at the [Event Partner’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) discretion |
| [<T7>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t7) | [Fields](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) at an event must be consistent with each other |
| [<T8>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t8) | [Qualification Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#qualificationmatch) will occur according to the official [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) schedule |
| [<T9>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t9) | Each [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) will be scheduled [Qualification Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#qualificationmatch) as follows |
| [<T10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t10) | [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) are ranked by their average [Qualification Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#qualificationmatch) scores |
| [<T11>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t11) | [Qualification Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#qualificationmatch) tiebreakers |
| [<T12>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t12) | How [Alliances](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance) are formed for [Teamwork Challenge](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#teamworkchallenge) [Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) |
| [<T13>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t13) | [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) playing in [Finals Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch) |
| [<T14>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t14) | [Finals Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch) schedule |
| [<T15>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t15) | [Robot Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch) schedule |
| [<T16>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t16) | No requirement that Skills [Fields](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) have the same modifications as Teamwork [Fields](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) |
| [<T17>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t17) | Skills rankings at events |
| [<T18>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t18) | Skills rankings globally |
| [<T19>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t19) | Robot Skills at league events |

* * *

**# Section 1 - Introduction**

## Overview

This section provides an introduction to the VEX IQ Robotics Competition (VIQRC) and VIQRC Mix & Match.

## The VEX IQ Robotics Competition

The world around us is constantly changing, and so are the ways we learn. Traditional classroom methods don’t always capture the hands-on problem solving and collaboration that are essential in STEM fields. Competitive robotics provides an alternative approach—one that engages [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) in real-world applications of engineering, coding, and design. Instead of just reading about these concepts, you get to experience them firsthand as you test ideas, refine solutions, and work as part of a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) to overcome challenges. By combining creativity with technical skills, the VEX IQ Robotics Competition helps make STEM learning more dynamic, practical, and inspiring.

Competitive robotics isn’t just about building a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot)—it’s about learning to approach challenges with confidence, resilience, and teamwork. The same problem-solving mindset that helps you design and refine a VEX [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) is the foundation for tackling real-world engineering problems, scientific breakthroughs, and technological innovations. Mix & Match is more than just a game—it’s an opportunity to develop skills that will shape the problem solvers and innovators of tomorrow.

Working together with other people—whether it be your own teammates or someone from another organization—can be challenging, but it’s just as much a part of the VEX Robotics Competition as building a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).

Within this manual, you’ll find the rules that define Mix & Match. These rules are designed to create a competitive yet fair environment that rewards creativity, strategy, and collaboration. Just like in the real world, constraints exist to challenge you—not to limit your potential, but to inspire innovative solutions.

As you embark on this season, remember that every challenge is an opportunity to grow. Whether you’re fine-tuning your design, refining your strategy, or working through unexpected setbacks, the lessons you learn here will stay with you far beyond the competition [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field).

Good luck, and we look forward to seeing your creativity and innovation in action!

Sincerely,

The VEX Robotics Game Design Committee, composed of members from VEX Robotics, the Robotics Education & Competition Foundation, and DWAB Technology

* * *

## VEX IQ Robotics Competition Mix & Match: A Primer

VEX IQ Robotics Competition Mix & Match is played on a 6’x8’ rectangular [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), set up as illustrated in the figures throughout this game manual.

The primary objectives of the game are to build [Stacks](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) out of [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) and [Beams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#beam), and [Place](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#placed) [Stacks](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) in [Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal). Additional [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) are introduced to the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) by [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) at the [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone). Points are awarded based on how many [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) and [Beams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#beam) are [Connected](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#connected), how many colors are included in each [Stack](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack), and for [Stacks](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) that match the color of the [Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal).

In the [Teamwork Challenge](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#teamworkchallenge), an [Alliance](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance) composed of two (2) [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) works together to score as many points as possible in a 60-second [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

[Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may also compete in [Robot Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch), where one (1) [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) tries to score as many points as possible with a slightly different set of rules. See Section 4 for more information.

The REC Library article titled “ [How to Navigate a Game Manual](https://viqrc-kb.recf.org/hc/en-us/articles/16455335249943-How-to-Navigate-a-Game-Manual)” describes the conventions and organizational structure used in this game manual, and may help you understand and interpret this Game Manual.

Note: The illustrations in this section of the Game Manual are intended to provide a general visual understanding of the game. Some figures may highlight or change the appearance of certain Field and Scoring Elements to emphasize or clarify intent.

[Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) should refer to official [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) specifications, found in Appendix A, for exact [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) dimensions, a full Field bill of materials, and exact details of [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) construction.

![](https://content.vexrobotics.com/docs/25-26/viqrc-mix-and-match/online-manual/images/SideView.png)

Figure O-1: Starting configuration of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) for a VEX IQ Robotics Competition Mix & Match Teamwork [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

* * *

## About the Game Manual - A Note from the GDC

This Game Manual and its appendices contain everything there is to know about this season’s game, VIQRC Mix & Match. It is intended to be a resource for all [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), [Head Referees](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee), [Event Partners](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner), and other members of the VIQRC community.

The rules contained in the following pages can be thought of as “constraints” that define this game, just as engineers begin any design project by defining their constraints. At the beginning of a season, constraints are all we have. We don’t know what the winning [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), best strategy, or most-frequently-violated rule will be any more than you do. Isn’t that exciting?

When exploring a new game, please approach this Game Manual with that mentality of looking at rules as constraints. The Game Manual, its appendices - and the official Q&A on RobotEvents.com - contain the full and complete list of constraints that are available for competitors to strategize, design, and build their [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).

Obviously, all [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) must adhere to these rules, and any stated intents of these rules. However, beyond that, there is no “right” way to play. There are no hidden restrictions, assumptions, or intended interpretations beyond what is written here. So it is up to you, the competitor, to find the path through these constraints that best suits your [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) goals and ambitions.

![](https://content.vexrobotics.com/docs/25-26/viqrc-mix-and-match/online-manual/images/Iso.png)

Figure O-2: Starting configuration of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) for a VEX IQ Robotics Competition Mix & Match Teamwork [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

* * *

## Our Intent - How We Want the Game to be Played

The [Game Design Committee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gdc) (GDC) carefully crafts each VEX IQ Robotics Competition game with a clear vision of how we believe it should be played. The GDC envisions Mix & Match as an execution-based challenge where [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) must collaborate effectively to maximize their scoring potential. The game pieces that are easiest for one [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) to obtain are the hardest for the other. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) are encouraged to plan ahead, and work with their partners to develop strategies that help each other gain access to all of the game pieces on the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field). With incentives for creating specific patterns, success in Mix & Match depends on both the quality and quantity of [Stacks](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack)—not one at the expense of the other. This design promotes continuous engagement, adaptability, and shared strategy. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) will have to work together to ensure the highest possible score.

As the season progresses and [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) develop new strategies, certain aspects of gameplay may evolve in ways that were not initially anticipated. To ensure that the game remains fair, competitive, and aligned with its original intent, the GDC has identified key areas that may be subject to clarification or adjustment throughout the season. While updates are not limited to these areas, the GDC believes these are some of the most critical for maintaining the integrity of gameplay:

- Game Piece Layout: The GDC has intentionally designed the Teamwork [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) layout to spread the game pieces out, and make one color of [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) for each [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) harder to obtain. We reserve the right to adjust the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) layout in Major Game Manual Updates if the layout does not properly disperse game pieces around the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field).
- Match Loading: Match [Loading](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#load) is still a new concept for VEX IQ Robotics Competition. The GDC feels like the rules regarding Match [Loading](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#load) clearly explains our intent that Match [Loading](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#load) should be one at a time, and that each game piece is released at rest before a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) picks it up. If Match [Loading](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#load) rules are being abused, we will make this process more strict and the [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) more punitive.
- Beams & Goals: The four (4) types of [Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal) provide varying levels of difficulty based on [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) location, heights to overcome, and the challenge of filling them to capacity. If we find that the more challenging types of [Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal) are underutilized throughout the season, we may add new bonus opportunities (or increase existing bonuses) to incentivize using these [Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal).

Any potential adjustments would be made with the goal of ensuring that the game plays as intended for the duration of the season. While we will try our best to adhere to the self-imposed limits on change per update, we may make larger/broader changes if it is deemed absolutely necessary. Any updates will be communicated through official rule updates.

* * *

**# Updates**

This manual will have a series of “major” and “minor” updates over the course of the season. Each version is official and must be used in official VIQRC events until the release of the next version, upon which the previous version becomes void.

The latest version of the Game Manual can always be found at:

[https://link.vex.com/docs/25-26/viqrc-mixandmatch-manual](https://link.vex.com/docs/25-26/viqrc-mixandmatch-manual).

Known major release dates are as follows:

|     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Release Date | Effective Date | Version # | Details |
| May 14, 2025 | May 14, 2025 | Version 0.1 | Initial game release |
| May 27, 2025 | May 27, 2025 | N/A | Official Q&A system opens |
| June 5, 2025 | June 12, 2025 | Version 0.2 | Minor typographical errors or formatting issues found in the initial release. Very few rule changes are expected. |
| June 26, 2025 | July 3, 2025 | Version 1.0 | May include gameplay or rule changes inspired by input from the official Q&A system and the VEX community. |
| August 7, 2025 | August 14, 2025 | Version 1.1 | Clarification / minor update |
| September 4, 2025 | September 11, 2025 | Version 2.0 | May include gameplay or rule changes inspired by early-season events. |
| October 9, 2025 | October 16, 2025 | Version 2.1 | Clarification / minor update |
| December 4, 2025 | December 11, 2025 | Version 2.2 | Clarification / minor update |
| January 29, 2026 | February 5, 2026 | Version 3.0 | May include gameplay or rule changes inspired by mid-season events. |
| April 2, 2026 | April 9, 2026 | Version 4.0 | May include gameplay or rule changes pertaining specifically to the VEX Robotics World Championship |

In addition to these known major updates, there may also be unscheduled updates released throughout the season if deemed critical by the GDC.

Any scheduled or unscheduled updates will always be released on a Thursday, no later than 5:00 PM CST (11:00 PM GMT). These updates will be announced via the VEX Forum, automatically pushed to the VIQRC Hub app, and shared via VEX Robotics / REC Foundation social media & email marketing channels. Once announced, the new version of the Game Manual will be immediately available at the link above.

Generally, Mix & Match Game Manual updates, scheduled or unscheduled, will include a grace period before the updated rules go into effect for competitions. See the Release Table above for specific dates. This grace period does not apply to the Version 0.1 Release, which serves as the initial rule set for the season. Any events that begin before the 7-day grace period has ended must continue using the rules from the previous Game Manual Release. This policy ensures fairness and consistency, allowing [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) to adapt their strategies and gameplay accordingly before the changes are enforced in official competitions.

During the 7-day grace period, the previous manual version will be available at [https://link.vex.com/docs/25-26/docs/25-26/viqrc-mixandmatch-manual-obsolete](https://link.vex.com/docs/25-26/docs/25-26/viqrc-mixandmatch-manual-obsolete). This link will be only be active during the grace period following each manual update, and will be disabled once it ends.

The GDC reserves the right to enforce critical updates to the Game Manual as effective immediately upon release, if we feel that the changes are critical for competitive integrity, safety, and/or other extenuating circumstances.

Multi-week league events (or similar) that cross over a grace period must use the version of the Game Manual that is in effect at the beginning of each league session. Leagues must update to new versions of the Game Manual between sessions as appropriate.

* * *

**# The Q&A System**

When first reviewing a new robotics game, it is natural to have questions about situations which may not be immediately clear. Navigating the Game Manual and seeking out answers to these questions is an important part of learning a new game. In many cases, the answer may just be in a different place than you first thought—or, if there is no rule explicitly prohibiting a gameplay strategy, then that usually means it is legal!

However, if a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is still unable to find an answer to their question after closely reviewing the relevant rules, then every [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) has the opportunity to ask for official rules interpretations in the [VEX Robotics Question & Answer System](https://www.robotevents.com/VIQRC/2025-2026/QA). These questions may be posted by an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) via the RobotEvents account that is associated with that [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).

All responses in this Q&A system should be treated as official rulings from the VEX Robotics Game Design Committee, and they represent the correct and official interpretation of the VEX Robotics Competition Rules. The Q&A system is the only source besides the Game Manual for official rulings and clarifications, and is functionally an extension of the Game Manual. Q&A rulings are effective immediately upon release.

The VEX IQ Robotics Competition Question & Answer System will open on May 27th, 2025.

Before posting on the Q&A system, be sure to review the [Q&A Usage Guidelines](https://www.robotevents.com/VIQRC/2025-2026/QA/guidelines):

1. Read and search the Game Manual before posting.
2. Read and search existing Q&As before posting.
3. Quote the applicable rule from the latest version of the Game Manual in your question.
4. Make a separate post for each question.
5. Use specific and appropriate question titles.
6. Questions will (mostly) be answered in the order they were received.
7. This system is the only source for official rules clarifications.

If there are any conflicts between the English-language PDF of the Game Manual and other supplemental or translated materials (e.g., referee training materials, the VIQRC Hub app, the game reveal video, a translated game manual, etc.), the most current version of the English-language PDF of the Game Manual takes precedence.

Similarly, it can never be assumed that definitions, rules, or other materials from previous seasons apply to the current game. Q&A responses from previous seasons are not considered official rulings for the current game. Any relevant clarifications that are needed should always be re-asked in the current season’s Q&A.

* * *

**# Additional Policies**

The rules and guidelines in these official documents and policies apply to [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) and events in the VEX Robotics Competitions alongside the rules in this Game Manual.

- [Code of Conduct](https://viqrc-kb.recf.org/hc/en-us/articles/9778593540247-Code-of-Conduct) \- Outlines the expectations of behavior and ethical standards for all attendees at REC Foundation-sanctioned events.
- [Student-Centered Policy](https://viqrc-kb.recf.org/hc/en-us/articles/9778591033879-Student-Centered-Policy) \- Communicates the REC Foundation’s goal of maximizing learning opportunities for [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student), and the mandate that [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) use designs, code, and game strategies that are consistent with their abilities and knowledge. The related Important Behavior Guidelines for [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) [Adults](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) provides guidelines for [Adults](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) to promote [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student)-centeredness when interacting with [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).
- [Commitment to Coach Excellence](https://viqrc-kb.recf.org/hc/en-us/articles/22840387244695-Commitment-to-Coach-Excellence) \- Communicates the partnership and expectations between the REC Foundation and Coaches. Must be agreed to during [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) registration.
- [Commitment to Event Excellence](https://kb.roboticseducation.org/hc/en-us/articles/12094736701975-Commitment-to-Event-Excellence) \- Communicates the partnership and expectations between the REC Foundation and [Event Partners](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner), with the goal of providing [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) with quality and uniform competition experiences throughout our programs.
- [Guide to Judging](https://kb.roboticseducation.org/hc/en-us/articles/4788499711127-Guide-to-Judging-Introduction-and-Terms) \- Provides policies and procedures for the judging process, and guidelines for [Teams’](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) engineering notebooks.
- [Organizational Policy](https://kb.roboticseducation.org/hc/en-us/articles/8077857213591-REC-Foundation-Organizational-Policy) \- Provides guidelines for organization and [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) numbers that are assigned during [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) registration.
- [Qualifying Criteria](https://kb.roboticseducation.org/hc/en-us/articles/5474199602071-Qualifying-Criteria-for-VEX-Robotics-Competition-Events) \- Provides the criteria that [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) and events must meet to qualify for Event Region Championships and the VEX Robotics World Championship.
- [Youth Protection Policy](https://viqrc-kb.recf.org/hc/en-us/articles/21020264309399-REC-Foundation-Youth-Protection-Policy) \- Provides information, guidelines, and procedures to create safe environments for participants in our range of programs.

* * *

**# Section 2 - The Game**

**# Field Overview**

The VEX IQ Robotics Competition Mix & Match [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) consists of the following:

- 36 [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin)




  - 10 blue [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin)




    - 1 [Preload](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#preload)
    - 6 that can be introduced through the blue [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone)
    - 3 that start in the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field)
  - 10 red [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin)




    - 1 [Preload](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#preload)
    - 6 that can be introduced through the red [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone)
    - 3 that start in the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field)
  - 16 orange [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) that start on the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field)
- Two (2) [Beams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#beam)
- One (1) [Floor Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floorgoal)
- Two (2) [Square Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#squaregoal), one red and one blue
- Two (2) < [Triangle Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#trianglegoal), one red and one blue
- One (1) [Standoff Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#standoffgoal)
- Two (2) [Load Zones](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone), one red and one blue
- Four (4) [Starting Pin Supports](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#startingpinsupport)

![](https://content.vexrobotics.com/docs/25-26/viqrc-mix-and-match/online-manual/images/TopView.png)

Figure FO-1 Starting configuration of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) for a VEX IQ Robotics Competition Mix & Match Teamwork Match.

![](https://content.vexrobotics.com/docs/25-26/viqrc-mix-and-match/online-manual/images/FO-2-100125-Anno.png)

Figure FO-2 Starting configuration of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) for a VEX IQ Robotics Competition Mix & Match Teamwork Match.A VIQRC Mix & Match [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), with Field Elements highlighted. < [Triangle Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#trianglegoal) (green), [Square Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#squaregoal) (yellow), [Starting Pin Supports](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#startingpinsupport) (blue), [Floor Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floorgoal) and [Standoff Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#standoffgoal) (orange), and [Load Zones](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone) (pink).

![](https://content.vexrobotics.com/docs/25-26/viqrc-mix-and-match/online-manual/images/DriverLayout.png)

Figure FO-3 The recommended locations for [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) and [Head Referees](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) during [Teamwork Challenge](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#teamworkchallenge) [Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

* * *

**# General Definitions**

Adult \- Anyone who is not a [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) or another defined term (e.g., [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee)).

Alliance \- A pre-assigned grouping of two (2) [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) that are paired together during a given [Teamwork Challenge](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#teamworkchallenge) [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

Alliance Score \- Points scored in a [Teamwork Challenge](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#teamworkchallenge) [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) that are awarded to both [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).

Disablement \- A penalty applied to a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) for a safety [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation). During [Disablement](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disablement), a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is no longer allowed to operate their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), and the [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) will be asked to place their Controller down. A [Disablement](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disablement) is not the same as a [Disqualification](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification).

Disqualification \- A penalty applied to a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) for a rule [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) (see [<GG6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg6) for more details). If a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) receives a [Disqualification](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification) in a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), the [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) will notify the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) of their [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) at the end of the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). At the [Head Referee’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) discretion, repeated [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) and/or [Disqualifications](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification) for a single [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may lead to its [Disqualification](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification) for the entire event.

Driver \- A [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) member who stands in the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) and is responsible for operating and controlling that [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot). Up to two [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) members may fulfill this role in a given [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) (see [<GG1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg1)), and there is no requirement that the same [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) serve as [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) in multiple [Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

Driver Station \- A region beside the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) where the [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) must remain during their [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) unless legally interacting with their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot). The [Driver Stations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) are represented by the red and blue lines in Figure FO-3.

Drive Team Members \- The two [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) and one Loader who participate in a given [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) as representatives of their [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team). No [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) may fill more than one role on a Drive Team in the same [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

- [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) 1 - Drives the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) until the mid- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) Driver switch (see [<GG11>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg11))
- Driver 2 - Drives the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) after the mid- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) Driver switch (see [<GG11>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg11))
- Loader - Introduces [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) into the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) for the whole [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match)

Field \- The entire playing [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), being six (6) [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) tiles wide by eight (8) [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) tiles long (totaling forty-eight (48) [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) tiles), including the [Field Perimeter](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldperimeter).

Field Element \- The [Field Perimeter](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldperimeter), [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor), PVC pipes, and VEX IQ pieces which comprise and/or are attached to the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field).

Field Perimeter \- The outer part of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), made up of four (4) outside corners and twenty-four (24) straight sections.

Floor \- The interior flat part of the playing [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), made up of the forty-eight (48) [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) tiles that are within the [Field Perimeter](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldperimeter).

Game Design Committee (GDC) \- The creators of VIQRC Mix & Match, and authors of this Game Manual. The GDC is the only official source for rules clarifications and Q&A responses; see Section 1.

License Plate \- A physical component on the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) that displays the [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) VEX IQ Robotics Competition number. Each [License Plate](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#licenseplate) must have a length and height of 3.5” x 1.5” (88.9mm x 38.1mm) and must not exceed a width of 0.25” (6.35mm) per [<R6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r6).

Match \- A set time period, consisting of [Autonomous Periods](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomousperiod) and/or [Driver Controlled Periods](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#drivercontrolledperiod), during which [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) play a defined version of Mix & Match to earn points. See Sections 3 & 4.

- Autonomous Period \- A time period during which [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) operate and react only to sensor inputs and/or commands pre-programmed by the [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) into the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) control system.
- Driver Controlled Period \- A time period during which [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) operate their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).

|     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) Type | Participants | [Autonomous Period](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomousperiod) (m:ss) | [Driver Controlled Period](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#drivercontrolledperiod) (m:ss) |
| [Teamwork Challenge](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#teamworkchallenge) | One [Alliance](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance), on one [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), made up of two [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), each with one [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) | None | 1:00 |
| [Driving Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#drivingskillsmatch) | One [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), with one [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) | None | 1:00 |
| [Autonomous Coding Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch) | One [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), with one [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) | 1:00 | None |

Robot \- A machine that has passed inspection, designed by [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) members to execute one or more tasks autonomously and/or by remote control from [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver).

Student \- Anyone born after May 1, 2010 (i.e., who will be 15 or younger at VEX Worlds 2026). Eligibility may also be granted based on a disability that has delayed education by at least one year. [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) are the individuals who design, build, repair, and program the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) with minimal [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) assistance.

- Elementary School Student – Any [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) born after May 1, 2013 (i.e., who will be 12 or younger at VEX Worlds 2026). [Elementary School Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#elementaryschoolstudent) may “play up” and compete as [Middle School Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#middleschoolstudent).
- Middle School Student \- Any eligible [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) that is not an [Elementary School Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#elementaryschoolstudent).

Team \- Three or more [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) make up a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team). To participate in an official VEX IQ Robotics Competition event, a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) must first register on RobotEvents.com and receive a VEX IQ Robotics Competition [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) number. A [Team's](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) unique number identifies their organization and their [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) within that organization. Each [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) must build their own [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), create their own code, and maintain their own Engineering Notebook if they choose to use one.

- A [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is classified as an Elementary School [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) if all members are [Elementary School Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#elementaryschoolstudent).
- A [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is classified as a Middle School [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) if any member is a [Middle School Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#middleschoolstudent), or if the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is made up of [Elementary School Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#elementaryschoolstudent) who declare themselves as “playing up” as [Middle School Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#middleschoolstudent) by registering their [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) as a Middle School [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).
- Once a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) has competed in an event as a Middle School [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), that [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may not change to an Elementary School [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) for the remainder of the season. If a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) mistakenly registers as an Elementary School [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) but is ineligible for that age group, their registration may be revised mid-season with RSM assistance; all prior qualifications for the season will be lost.
- [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may be associated with schools, community/youth organizations, or a group of neighborhood [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student).

In the context of this Game Manual, [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) contain three types of [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) roles related to [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) build, design, and coding. See [<G2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g2) and [<G5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g5) for more information. [Adults](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) may not fulfill any of these roles.

- Builder \- The [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student)(s) on the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) who assemble(s) the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot). [Adults](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) are permitted to teach the [Builder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#builder)(s) associated concepts, but should never work on the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).
- Coder \- The [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student)(s) on the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) who write(s) the computer code that is downloaded onto the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot). [Adults](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) are permitted to teach the [Coder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#coder)(s) associated concepts, but should never work on the code that goes on the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).
- Designer \- The [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student)(s) on the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) who design(s) the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) to be built for competition. [Adults](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) are permitted to teach the [Designer](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#designer)(s) associated concepts, but should never work on the design of the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).

Violation \- The act of breaking a rule in the Game Manual.

- Minor Violation \- A [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) which does not result in a [Disqualification](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification).




  - Accidental, momentary, or otherwise non- [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting) [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) are usually [Minor Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation).
  - [Minor Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation) usually result in a verbal notification from the [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) during the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), which should serve to inform the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) that a rule is being Violated before it escalates to a [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation).
- Major Violation \- A [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) which results in a [Disqualification](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification).




  - Unless otherwise noted in a rule, all [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting) [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) are [Major Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation).
  - If noted in the rule, egregious or strategic [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) or intentional actions that result in [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) may also be [Major Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation).
  - Multiple [Minor Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation) within a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) or tournament may escalate to a [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) at the [Head Referee’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) discretion or as specified in a rule.
- Score Affecting \- A [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) which improves an [Alliance’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance) score at the end of a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).




  - Multiple [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) within a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) can cumulatively become [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting).
  - When evaluating whether a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) was [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting), [Head Referees](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) will focus primarily on any [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) actions that were directly related to the [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation).
  - Determining whether a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) was [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting) can only be done once the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) is complete and the scores have been calculated. [Minor Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation) carry over into [Finals Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch) unless otherwise specified within a rule.
- CoC-related Violation \- A [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of a rule that relates to the RECF Code of Conduct and related processes. For VIQRC, the included rules are: [<S2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#s2), [<G1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g1), [<G2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g2), [<G4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g4), [<G5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g5), [<R1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r1) through [<R4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r4), and [Major Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) of [<S1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#s1).




  - Potential [CoC-related Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) should be brought to the attention of the [Event Partner](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner), and resolved through the Code of Conduct Reporting Process in coordination with the [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting), [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee), Judge Advisor, and RECF Regional Support Manager. Follow-up investigations are conducted by the RECF Rules & Conduct Committee (RCC). Penalties for confirmed [CoC-related Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) can range from single- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) [Disqualifications](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification) to removal from the program.

Some rules include [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) Notes in red italicized text to denote special circumstances or provide additional clarifications. If no [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) Notes are found in a given rule, then it should be assumed that the default definitions above apply.

To determine whether a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) may have been [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting), check whether the [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) directly contributed to increasing the score of the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). If it did not increase the [Alliance’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance) score, then the [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) was not [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting), and it was very likely a [Minor Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation).

See the flowcharts in figures V-1, V-2, and V-3 for more information, and [this article](https://kb.roboticseducation.org/hc/en-us/articles/14490397054359-Code-of-Conduct-Reporting-Process) for full details of the event CoC process.

![A flowchart used to determine iolations during Robot inspection](https://content.vexrobotics.com/docs/25-26/v5rc-push-back/online-manual/images/V-1-Flowchart-1125.png)

Figure V-1: The process for determining [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) during [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) inspection.

![A flowchart used to determine whether infractions should be considered a Violation](https://content.vexrobotics.com/docs/25-26/viqrc-mix-and-match/online-manual/images/Violation-Flowchart-100625.png)

Figure V-2:The process for determining whether or not an infraction should result in a [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) or [Minor Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation)

![A flowchart used to ddetermining CoC-related Violations](https://content.vexrobotics.com/docs/25-26/v5rc-push-back/online-manual/images/V-3-Flowchart-112625.png)

Figure V-3: The process for determining [CoC-related Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation)

* * *

**# Game-Specific Definitions**

Connected \- A [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) status. See [<SC3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc3).

Cleared \- A [Starting Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#startingpin) status. See [<SC7>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sc7).

Goal \- A place where [Stacks](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) can be [Placed](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#placed). There are four (4) varieties of [Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal) in VIQRC Mix & Match:

- Square Goal \- A segment of the [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor) in a corner of the long side of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) opposite from the audience. Each [Square Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#squaregoal) is bordered by the inside of the [Field Perimeter](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldperimeter) and the inside edges of the VEX IQ pieces connected to the [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor). Each [Square Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#squaregoal) has a color, red or blue, determined by its VEX IQ pieces and PET sheet. Each [Square Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#squaregoal) can hold a maximum of one (1) [Placed](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#placed) [Stack](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack).
- Floor Goal \- A segment of the [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor) in the center of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) surrounding the [Standoff Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#standoffgoal). The [Floor Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floorgoal) is defined by the center, white-outlined portion of the PET sheet connected to the [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor) underneath the [Standoff Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#standoffgoal), and includes that white line.
