[Adults](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) should not make decisions about the [Robot’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) build, design, or gameplay, and should not provide an unfair advantage by providing ‘help’ that is beyond the [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student)’ independent abilities. [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) must be prepared to demonstrate an active understanding of their [Robot’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) design, construction, and programming to judges or event staff. [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) should build, design, and code the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) with minimal [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) involvement.

Some amount of [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) mentorship, teaching, and/or guidance is an expected and encouraged facet of VEX competitions. No one is born an expert in robotics! However, obstacles should always be viewed as teaching opportunities, not problems for an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) to solve for the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).

When building or designing the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), it is…

- Okay for an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) to help a [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) consider why something failed, so it can be improved.
- Not okay for an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) to provide step by step instructions or photos for the [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) to copy.

When a mechanism falls off, it is…

- Okay for an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) to help a [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) consider why it failed, so it can be improved.
- Not okay for an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) to investigate or put the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) back together.

When a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) encounters a complex programming concept, it is…

- Okay for an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) to guide a [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) through a flowchart to understand its logic.
- Not okay for an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) to write a premade command for that [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) to copy / paste.

During [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) play, it is…

- Okay for an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) to provide cheerful, positive encouragement as a spectator.
- Not okay for an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) to explicitly shout step-by-step commands from the audience.

This rule operates in tandem with the [REC Foundation Student Centered Policy](https://viqrc-kb.recf.org/hc/en-us/articles/9778591033879-Student-Centered-Policy), which is available in the REC Library for [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) to reference throughout the season.

Violation Notes: Potential [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule will be reviewed on a case-by-case basis. By definition, all [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule become [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting) as soon as a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) which was built or programmed by an [Adult](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) scores points in a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). All reported and/or suspected [<G2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g2) [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) should be reported to the [Event Partner](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) during the event, and should be reported to the REC Foundation Rules and Conduct Committee following the event.

##### <G3>

<G3>Use common sense. When reading and applying the various rules in this document, please remember that common sense always applies in the VEX IQ Robotics Competition.

Some examples may include:

- If there is an obvious typographical error (such as “per [<T5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t5)” instead of “per [<GG5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg5)”), this does not mean that the error should be taken literally until corrected in a future update.
- Understand the realities of the VEX IQ [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) construction system. For example, if a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) could hover above the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) for a whole [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), that would create loopholes in many of the rules. But… they can’t. So… don’t worry about it.
- When in doubt, if there is no rule prohibiting an action, it is generally legal. However, if you have to ask whether a given action would violate [<S1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#s1), [<G1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g1), or [<T1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t1) then that’s probably a good indication that it is outside the spirit of the competition. On the other hand, if there’s not a rule that makes a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) part legal, it’s not allowed.
- In general, [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) will be given the “benefit of the doubt” in the case of accidental or edge-case rules infractions. However, there is a limit to this allowance, and repeated or strategic infractions will still be penalized.

##### <G4>

<G4>All work must represent the skill level of the Students on the Team. The [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) design, [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), coding, strategy, and ongoing work must represent the skill level of the [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) currently on the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).

- [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) must avoid academic dishonesty and should not copy a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) or mechanism that has been provided for them. This includes, but is not limited to, the use of instructions, pictures & videos, notebooks, CAD designs, and/or any other documentation useful to the design process provided by anyone that is not a [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) on the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) (including [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) on another [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team)).
- [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may be inspired by designs by other [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), and use an idea from someone else to spark innovation, but are expected to document and demonstrate this in their engineering notebook alongside evidence of iteration. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) are required to present this evidence if asked to do so by a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) inspector, [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee), [Event Partner](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner), or Judge.

  - Using elements of another design as a starting point is acceptable if the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is capable of demonstrating evidence of iteration, innovation, and/or modification that makes the design uniquely their own. Documentation should clearly demonstrate the idea that was used for inspiration, and how it was changed for the final implementation on the [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot). It should be clear that this final implementation is not an exact copy of ANY other original design.
  - Failure to demonstrate evidence of iteration, innovation, and/or modification will result in a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation).

- [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may use [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) plans and code (e.g., the annual Hero Bot, VEXcode configurations, etc.) provided by VEX Robotics or the RECF, but are encouraged to use these [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), mechanisms, and code only as a starting point that [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) modify, improve, or replace as their skills increase. Plans provided by VEX Robotics or the RECF are the only legal plans available for use in competition.
- This rule still applies to [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) within the same school, organization, or club. [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) and/or code sets that are identical or substantially similar to one another across [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) within the same school/organization/club will be considered in [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule, regardless of whether they compete in the same or different events. Clause D does not apply in situations where both/all [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) are using the unmodified Hero Bot design, as allowed by clause C of this rule.

For more information, including acceptable and unacceptable examples of mechanical design, construction, coding, and strategy solutions, please refer to the [Student Centered Policy](https://kb.roboticseducation.org/hc/en-us/articles/5449868745367-Student-Centered-Policy) in the RECF Library.

The VEX Robotics Competition and the Robotics Education & Competition Foundation (RECF) recognize that many third-party individuals and organizations produce and distribute [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) designs, instructions, and/or other materials that are not under our direct control. We cannot legally regulate or restrict the activities of these external entities. However, when [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) use these resources in ways that violate the spirit and letter of the VEX Robotics Game Manual—particularly Rules [<G2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g2) and [<G4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g4)—they undermine the core mission of the program: to provide [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) with hands-on opportunities to learn, design, and innovate.

While it is never our intent to punish [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student), we can legally regulate and restrict the activities of the [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) in our competitions, and we must preserve the fairness, educational value, and integrity of the competition. Therefore, [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) found to be in [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of these rules will be held accountable to the strictest interpretations of [<G2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g2) and [<G4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g4).

It is the responsibility of each [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) to be able to explain and defend the design, construction, and programming of their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) if questioned by referees, inspectors, [Event Partners](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner), or judges. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) should be prepared to describe their design process, justify design decisions, and demonstrate a full understanding of how their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) and code function.

**If a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is unable, for any reason, to provide reasonable evidence (when requested by event staff) that their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) and code are the result of their own work, it is appropriate to assume that the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is in [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of [<G2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g2) and/or [<G4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g4).**

Event organizers cannot reasonably know the origins of every design or independently verify whether a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) was created from scratch, purchased online, or copied from pictures of another [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) design. When questions of authenticity arise, the only direct and fair approach is to require [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) to explain and defend their work. This is not unlike academic honesty concerns in schools, and intellectual property concerns in business. By requiring [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) to defend their designs, we ensure that they are developing not only technical skills, but effective communication skills and accountability, as well.

Consequences may include disqualification from matches, removal from events, and/or escalation of the investigation to VEX Robotics and the RECF for further disciplinary action, which may include sanctions up to and including removal from the program.

Event staff should bear in mind [<G3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g3), and use common sense when enforcing this rule. It is not the intent to actively hunt for [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule, compare every [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) at an event to all other known [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) designs, or closely question every team at an event about their [Robot's](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) code. This rule is a set of tools for use if potential [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) are noted by or reported to event staff, and it is expected that most [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) will never be required to defend their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) design or code.

[Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) or individuals who deliberately weaponize, manipulate, or falsely report [<G4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g4) [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) for competitive gain or to harass another Team may be subject to a separate RECF Code of Conduct investigation. Misuse of this rule is considered a serious [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation).

Violation Notes:

  - [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) believed to be in [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule should be reported to the Judge Advisor, [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee), or [Event Partner](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) for further investigation in coordination with the RSM. Based on the investigation the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may be removed from further [Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), have their Robot Skills Challenge scores removed, and/or be removed from consideration from judged awards.
  - [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule will be evaluated on a case-by-case basis, in tandem with the RECF Student Centered Policy as noted in [<G2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g2), and the REC Foundation Code of Conduct as noted in [<G1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#winpoints). All reported and/or suspected [<G4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g4) [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) should be reported to the [Event Partner](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) during the event, and should be reported to the RECF Rules and Conduct Committee following the event.

##### <G5>

<G5>Each Student can only belong to one Team. Each Team must include [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers), [Coder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team)(s), [Designer](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team)(s), and [Builder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team)(s). Many also include notebooker(s). No [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) may fulfill any of these roles for more than one VEX IQ Robotics Competition [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) in a given competition season. [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) may have more than one role on the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), e.g., the [Designer](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may also be the [Builder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), the [Coder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), and a [Drive Team Member](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammember).

- [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) members may only move from one [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) to another for non-strategic reasons outside of the [Team's](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) control.

  - Examples of permissible moves may include, but are not limited to, changing schools, conflicts within a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), or combining/splitting [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).
  - Examples of strategic moves in [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule may include, but are not limited to, one [Coder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) “switching” [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) in order to program multiple [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), one [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) designing multiple teams’ [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), or one [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) writing the Engineering Notebook for multiple [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).
  - If a [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) leaves a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) to join another [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), [<G4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g4) still applies to the [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) remaining on the previous [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team). For example, if a [Coder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) leaves a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), then that [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) must still represent the skill level of the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) without that [Coder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team). One way to accomplish this would be to ensure that the [Coder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) teaches or trains a “replacement” [Coder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) in their absence.
  - Points ii and iii are intended to represent real-world situations that are found in industry engineering. If a vital member of a professional engineering team were to suddenly leave, the remaining members of the team should still be capable of working on / maintaining their project.

- When a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) qualifies for a Championship event (e.g., States, Nationals, Worlds, etc.) the [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) on the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) attending the Championship event are expected to be the same [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) on the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) that was awarded the spot. [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) can be added as support to the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), but may not be added as [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) or [Coders](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) for the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).
  - An exception is allowed if only one (1) member of the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is able to attend the event. The [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) can make a single substitution of a [Drive Team Member](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammember) or [Coder](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) for the Championship event with another [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student), even if that [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) has competed on a different [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team). This [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) will now be a member of this new [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) and may not substitute back to the original [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) during the season.

Note: [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) cannot “borrow” [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) from other [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) to serve as [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers), [Coders](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), [Designers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) and [Builders](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) or notebookers. However, [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) can add permanent members throughout the season under the guidelines of this rule.

Violation Notes: [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) believed to be in [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule should be reported to the Judge Advisor, [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee), or [Event Partner](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) for further investigation in coordination with the RSM.

[Event Partners](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) should bear in mind [<G3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g3), and use common sense when enforcing this rule. It is not the intent to punish a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) who may change [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) members over the course of a season due to illness, changing schools, conflicts within a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team), etc.

[Event Partners](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) and referees are not expected to keep a roster of any [Student](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) who has ever been a [Drive Team Member](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammember) for one day. This rule is intended to block any instance of loaning or sharing [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) members for the sole purpose of gaining a competitive advantage.

##### <GG1>

<GG1>Drivers drive your Robot, and stay in the Driver Station. During a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) may only be operated by that [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) and/or software running on the [Robot’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) control system. Each [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may send up to three (3) [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) to their [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) for a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match): two (2) [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) and one (1) Loader. Those [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) must remain in their [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation), except when legally interacting with their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) per [<GG10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg10).

1. [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) are prohibited from any of the following actions during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match):




1. Using any sort of communication device in the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation). Non-headphone devices with communication features turned off (e.g. a phone in airplane mode or a walkie talkie turned off) are allowed. If communication features are needed for translation apps during post- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) discussions, it should not be considered a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation).
2. Standing or sitting on any sort of object during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), regardless of whether the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) is on the [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor) or elevated, except as required by an official [accommodation request](https://kb.roboticseducation.org/hc/en-us/articles/22353712963095-Needs-based-Special-Accommodations) that has been approved by the REC Foundation.
3. Using additional materials to simplify the game challenge during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).
4. To ensure that [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) are aware of verbal calls during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) (as an application of rules [<T1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t1), [<G1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g1), [<S1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#s1), and [<G3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g3)), powered headphones, earbuds, and/or passive earpieces connected to electronic devices cannot be worn/used in the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) except as required by an official [accommodation request](https://kb.roboticseducation.org/hc/en-us/articles/22353712963095-Needs-based-Special-Accommodations) that has been approved by the REC Foundation.

Point iii is intended to refer to non- [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot)-related items that directly influence gameplay, such as using a ramp to assist with the [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone). Provided no other rules are violated, and the items do not pose any safety or [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) damage risks, the following examples are not considered [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of [<GG1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg1):

   - Materials used before or after a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), such as a pre- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) alignment aid
   - Strategic aids, such as a whiteboard or clipboard
   - Earplugs, gloves, or other personal accessories

4. Individuals who are not [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) for a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) cannot provide directions, commands, or advice to the [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) during that [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). They're welcome to provide cheerful, positive encouragement, but should not affect [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) play or strategy.

Note: [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) are the only [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) members that are allowed to be in the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). [Adults](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#adult) (other than event staff) are not permitted to be in the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

Violation Notes: [Major Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) of this rule are not required to be [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting), and could invoke [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of other rules, such as [<G1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g1), [<G2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g2), [<G5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g5), or [<GG11>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg11).

##### <GG2>

<GG2> A Team’s Robot should attend every Match. The [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) must report to the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) for the [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) assigned [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), even if the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) is not functional. If the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) is not at the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) for the entire duration of the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), that [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is considered a “no show” and will receive zero (0) points. The other [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) in the [Alliance](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance) will still play and receive points for the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

1. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) are expected to participate in all scheduled [Qualification Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#qualificationmatch) and, if they’re ranked high enough to be included in a Finals [Alliance](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance), [Finals Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch). Failure to attend scheduled [Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) may be considered a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of [<G1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g1) and the Code of Conduct. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) that participate in zero [Qualification Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#qualificationmatch) cannot be considered for Judged Awards.

##### <GG3>

<GG3>Robots on the field must be ready to play. When a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) puts their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) on the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), it must be prepared to play (i.e., batteries charged, sized within the starting size constraint, etc.).

1. [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) must be placed on the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) promptly. Repeated failure to do so could result in a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of [<G1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#g1) and/or removal of the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) from the current [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) at the [Head Referee’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) discretion.
2. If a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) is not placed on the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) prior to the start of a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), it cannot be placed on the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) during that [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

The definition of the word “promptly” is at the discretion of the [Event Partner](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) and [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee), who will consider event schedule, previous [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) or delays, etc. As a general guideline, five seconds to check [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) alignment would be acceptable, but five minutes to assemble multiple parts together would not.

##### <GG4>

<GG4>Hands out of the Field. During a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) are prohibited from making intentional contact with any [Field Element](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldelements), [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), or [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) that has been introduced to the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), except for the allowances in [<GG10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg10), [<RSC5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc5), and/or [<SG6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg6).

1. [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) are not permitted to reach into the 3-dimensional volume of the [Field Perimeter](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldperimeter) at any time during the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), apart from the actions described above. Rule [<S1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#s1); applies.
2. Transitive contact, such as contact with the [Field Perimeter](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldperimeter) that causes the [Field Perimeter](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldperimeter) to contact Field Elements or objects inside of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), could be considered a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule.

Note: Any concerns regarding [Field Element](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldelements) or [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) starting positions should be raised with the [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) prior to the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) members may never adjust [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) or Field Elements themselves.

If a [Drive Team Member's](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) hands extend over the Field and/or [Field Perimeter](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldperimeter) in a way that is safe and doesn’t contact anything in the Field, it’s unlikely to be a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation). However, [Head Referees](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) may still ask [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) to step back and remain completely outside the field when necessary (e.g., for safety reasons or to reduce the chances of gameplay interference).

##### <GG5>

<GG5>Match Replays are allowed, but rare. [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) replays (i.e., playing a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) over again from its start) are at the discretion of the [Event Partner](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) and [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee), and will only be issued in the most extreme circumstances. Some examples that may warrant a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) replay are as follows (note that this is not an exhaustive list):

1. [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting) “Field fault” issues.




1. [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) not being reset before the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) starts.
2. Field Elements detaching or moving beyond normal tolerances, not a result of [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) interactions.
2. [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting) game rule issues.




1. A [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) is reset before the score is determined.
2. A [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) is run before its scheduled time without a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).

##### <GG>

<GG6>Disqualifications. A [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) that is issued a [Disqualification](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification) in a [Qualification Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#qualificationmatch) receives zero (0) points for the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). The other [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) on their [Alliance](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance) will still receive points for the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

1. In [Finals Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch), [Disqualifications](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification) apply to the whole [Alliance](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance), not just one [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team). An [Alliance](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance) that receives a [Disqualification](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification) in a [Finals Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch) will receive zero (0) points.
2. A [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) that receives a [Disqualification](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification) in a [Robot Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch) will receive a score of zero (0).

##### <GG7>

<GG7>Timeouts. There are no timeouts in VIQRC tournaments.

##### <GG8>

<GG8>Keep your Robot together. [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) may not intentionally detach parts or leave mechanisms on the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) during any [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

1. Parts that become unintentionally detached from the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) are no longer considered to be part of the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) and can be either left on the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) or collected by a [Drive Team Member](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) during a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) reset using [<GG10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg10).

##### <GG9>

<GG9>Don’t damage the Field. [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) interactions which damage the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) or any Field Elements are prohibited. For the purpose of this rule, “damage” is defined as anything which requires repair in order to begin the next [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), such as causing part of a [Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal) to detach from the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field).

[Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) are responsible for the actions of their [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) at all times, especially when interacting with the [Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal). If a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) chooses to repeatedly ram full-speed into a [Field Element](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldelements), it will be hard to convince a [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) that any damage caused was “accidental.”

Violation Notes:

- In most cases, accidental [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) damage should only be considered a [Minor Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation)
- Egregious, intentional, or repeated accidental/ [Minor Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation) may escalate to a [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) at the [Head Referee’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) discretion

##### <GG10>

<GG10>Handling the Robot mid-match is allowed under certain circumstances. If a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) goes completely outside the playing [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), gets stuck, tips over, or otherwise requires assistance, the [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) may retrieve & reset their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot). To do so, the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) must do the following:

1. Signal the Referee by placing their VEX IQ Controller on the ground. The [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) may ask the [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) to demonstrate the problem using the Robot Controller before approving the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) reset (e.g., confirming that the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) is broken, undriveable, or stuck on an obstacle) if the issue with the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) isn't obvious.
2. Any [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) being controlled by the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) while being handled must be removed from the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), and can be returned by a Loader in accordance with [<SG4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg4). No other [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) should be moved or adjusted.




1. In the context of this rule, “controlled” implies that the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) was manipulating the [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject), and not simply touching it. For example, if the [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) would move with the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) either vertically or while turning, then the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) is “controlling” that [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject).
3. The [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) must be placed back into a legal position that meets the criteria listed in clauses a,b, c, & d of [<SG1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg1). If any [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) are preventing the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) from being legally placed, they should be removed from the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) and reintroduced by a Loader in accordance with [<SG4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg4). The [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) does not get a new [Preload](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#preload) [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) during this reset.
4. Swapping one set of parts for another, or adding new pieces to a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) mid- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) during a [<GG10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg10) or [<RSC5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc5) interaction is considered a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of the intent and spirit of this rule. Repairing a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), or reattaching parts of the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) that fall off during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), is allowed.
5. As described in rule [<S1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#s1), [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) cannot step into the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) at any time during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). If the [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) cannot reach the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) due to the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) being in the center of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), they may ask the [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) to pick up the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) and hand it to the [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) for placement according to the conditions above.


Violation Notes: This rule is intended to allow [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) to fix damaged [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) or help get their [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) “out of trouble.” Strategically exploiting this rule may be considered a [Minor Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation) or [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) at the [Head Referee’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) discretion.

##### <GG11>

<GG11>A Team’s two Drivers switch Controllers midway through the Match. In a given [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), up to two (2) [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) may be in the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) per [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team). The two [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) must switch their controller between thirty-five seconds (0:35 on the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) timer) and twenty-five seconds (0:25 on the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) timer) remaining in the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

1. No [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) shall operate a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) for more than thirty-five (35) seconds.
2. The second [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) may not touch their [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) controls until the controller is passed to them.
3. Once the controller is passed, the first [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) may no longer touch their [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) controls.
4. A [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) cannot also be a Loader in the same [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).
5. If a Drive Team for a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) only has two members, one must serve as the [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) until the mid- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) switch. The second [Drive Team Member](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) may serve as either the 2nd [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) (after the mid- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) switch) or the Loader for the full [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), but cannot fill both roles. If the 2nd [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) position is unfilled, the [Robot’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) operation (even prewritten commands) must cease after the first thirty-five (35) seconds of the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).
6. If only one [Drive Team Member](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) is present, the [Robot’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) operation (even prewritten commands) must cease after the first thirty-five (35) seconds of the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) and the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) will not have a Loader during that [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).


Violation Notes: At a minimum, any [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule is considered a [Minor Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation). Whether it escalates to a [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) or not is dependent upon the [Head Referee’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) judgment regarding:

- Prior [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation)
- Any [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting) actions that were a direct result of the [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation), such as the first [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) scoring additional points after 35 seconds of driving or a [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) also serving as a Loader in the same [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

##### <GG12>

<GG12>Don’t Start Before the Timer, and Stop Moving at the end of the Match. [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) inputs and [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) may not begin before the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) timer starts, and must cease at the end of the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), when the timer reaches 0:00.

1. A pre-programmed routine which causes [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) motion to start before the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) or continue after the end of the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) would violate this rule.
2. Any scoring which takes place after the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) due to [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) continuing to move will not count toward the score and is a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule.

It is expected that many Mix & Match [Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) will have last-second “buzzer-beater” moments. The key moment occurs when the timer display shows 0:00. At many events, a buzzer sound will also play at T=0:00; however, the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) timer display takes precedence in the event of any audio discrepancies.

If a [Stack](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) is released from a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) before this moment, it will be allowed to finish its path and the score will be calculated once it comes to rest. However, if it is released after this moment (i.e., the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) was still moving past T=0:00) it will not count and the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) will receive a [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) as described below.

In cases where a last-second scoring attempt is “too close to call,” [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) will generally be given the “benefit of the doubt” and the score will be counted. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) are advised to [Place](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#placed) and release [Stacks](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#stack) a second or two before the timer reaches zero to avoid the need for referee judgment calls.

Violation Notes:

- Because scoring that happens after the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) is not counted, all [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of [<GG12>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg12) should be recorded as [Minor Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation).
- If a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) receives three [Minor Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation) within the same event, all future [<GG12>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg12) [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) at that event will be considered [Major Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) and [Disqualifications](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification).
- This count does not reset for any reason within an event (e.g., Qualification vs [Finals Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch), one of the [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) “dropped score” [Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), etc.), but does not include [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) that occur in [Robot Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch)

##### <GG13>

<GG13>Ending a Match early. If an [Alliance](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#alliance) wants to end a [Qualification Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#qualificationmatch) or a [Finals Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch) early, both [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) must signal the referee by ceasing all [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) motion and placing their controllers on the ground. The referee will then signal to the [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) that the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) is over and will begin to tally the score. If the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) is a tiebreaker [Finals Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch) for first place, then the [Match Stop Time](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#matchstoptime) will also be recorded (see <T14b>).

##### <SG1>

<SG1>Starting a Match. At the beginning of a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) must be placed such that it meets all of the following criteria:

1. Fit within an 11” wide x 20” long x 15” high (279mm x 508mm x 381mm) volume, as checked during inspection per [<R5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#r5).
2. Not contacting any [Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal) other than the one specified in clause c, other [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), or [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) other than a maximum of one (1) [Preload](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#preload). See rule [<SG5>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg5).
3. Contacting the structure of one of the two < [Triangle Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#trianglegoal).




1. For Teamwork Challenge [Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) listed as [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) 1 (printed [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) list), listed as Red [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) (RobotEvents.com), or listed first (VEXvia) must place their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) in contact with the red [Triangle Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#trianglegoal).
2. For Teamwork Challenge [Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) listed as [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) 2 (printed [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) list), listed as Blue [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) (RobotEvents.com), or listed second (VEXvia) must place their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) in contact with the blue [Triangle Goal](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#trianglegoal).
4. Only be contacting the [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor) and the structure of the Goal.
5. Completely stationary (i.e., no motors or other mechanisms in motion) until the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) timer starts. Pre-charging a pneumatic system (i.e., having the Pneumatic Pump running prior to the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match)) is the only permitted exception to this rule.
6. The starting configuration of the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) at the beginning of a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) must be the same as a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) configuration that was checked during [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) inspection.


Violation Notes: The [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) will not begin with any conditions in this rule unmet. If a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) cannot meet these conditions in a timely manner, the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) will be removed from the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) and rules <R3d> and [<GG2>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg2) will apply until the situation is corrected. In most cases, they will not receive a [Disqualification](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification), but they will not be permitted to play in the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

##### <SG2>

<SG2>Horizontal expansion is limited. [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) cannot expand horizontally beyond the 11” x 20” starting size limit at any time in the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

##### <SG3>

<SG3>Vertical expansion is unlimited. Once the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) begins, [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) may expand vertically beyond the 15” starting size limit with no limits.

##### <SG4>

<SG4>Keep Scoring Objects in the Field. [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) that leave the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) may be reintroduced by a Loader in accordance with [<SG6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg6) with the following restrictions:

1. A blue [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) that leaves the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) may only be reintroduced by the blue Loader at the blue [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone); a red [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) that leaves the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) may only be reintroduced by the red Loader at the red [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone).
2. An orange [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) or [Beam](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#beam) that leaves the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) must be given to the Loader in the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) closest to where it left the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), and can only be reintroduced by that Loader.
3. “Leaving the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field)” means that a [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) is outside of the [Field Perimeter](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldperimeter), no longer in contact with the [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor) or Field Elements, and not supported by [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) or [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) that are still inside the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field).
4. If a [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) is removed from a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) during a [<GG10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg10) interaction, it is considered “out of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field)” as soon as it is no longer in contact with any [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).
5. If a [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) is on its way out of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) (as determined by the [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee)), but is deflected back into the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) by a [Drive Team Member](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers), field monitor, ceiling/wall, or other external factor, [<SG4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg4) would still apply. This [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) should be considered “out of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field),” removed by a [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee), and given to a Loader.
6. If a set of [Connected](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#connected) [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) leaves the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), they must be separated and reintroduced one at a time by the appropriate Loader(s).

Violation Note: [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) that are deemed by the [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) to be intentional or strategic should immediately escalate to a [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation).

##### <SG5>

<SG5>Each Robot gets one Pin as a Preload. For [Teamwork Challenge](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#teamworkchallenge) [Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) listed as [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) 1 (printed [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) list) or Red [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) (RobotEvents.com) will use a red [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin). [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) 2 / Blue [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) will use a blue [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin). Prior to the start of each [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), each [Preload](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#preload) must be placed such that it meets all of the following criteria:

1. Contacting exactly one [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).
2. Not contacting any Field Elements (excluding the [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor)), [Goals](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#goal), or other [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject).


If a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) is not present for a Teamwork Match, its [Preload](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#preload) should be placed in the matching [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone).

##### <SG6>

<SG6>Using the Load Zone. [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) may be [Loaded](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#load) through the [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone) during the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), must meet all of the following criteria:

1. Red and blue [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) may only be Loaded into the [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone) that matches the color of that [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin). [Beams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#beam) and/or orange [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) that leave the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) may be reintroduced at either [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone) as described in rule [<SG4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg4).
2. The [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) must be placed in contact with the VEX IQ beam attached to the [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor).
3. The Loader may only put a [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) into a [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone) if no other [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) are in contact with that [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone).
4. A [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) may not contact a [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) in the [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone) if that [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) is being contacted by a human.
5. Once a [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) is [Placed](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#placed) into a [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone) and released, it may no longer be contacted by a Loader.
6. If a [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) is introduced improperly (e.g., while another [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) is in contact with the [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone)), it must be retrieved by the Loader and reintroduced.
7. A Loaded [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) or [Beam](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#beam) must be placed in a stationary position, and must remain in contact with the VEX IQ beam after it is released by the Loader until it is contacted by a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) or another [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) that is being manipulated by a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).
8. [Pins](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) that begin the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) outside the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) cannot break the plane of the [Field Perimeter](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#fieldperimeter) until the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) begins.

Note: Although it is not required, [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) are highly recommended to remain some distance away from the [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) until the Loader’s hand has clearly been removed. This will make clauses d & e abundantly clear to [Head Referees](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee).

Violation Notes:

- [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) are responsible for their own actions. [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) that involve a Loader and [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) from opposite [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) will be given to both [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team).
- It is expected that most [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) of this rule will be accidental. In accidental cases that end up being [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting) (i.e., an illegally- [Loaded](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#load) [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) is [Connected](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#connected) to another [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject)), the first occurrence during a [Qualification Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#qualificationmatch) may be treated as a [Minor Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#minorviolation) and a “final notice” that any future [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) will result in [Disqualification](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#disqualification) for the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).
- Any [Score Affecting](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoreaffecting) [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) during a [Finals Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#finalsmatch) (accidental and intentional) must be treated as a [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation).
- Repeated, intentional, or egregious [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) may escalate to a [Major Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#majorviolation) at the [Head Referee’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) discretion. One example of an egregious [Violation](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation) would be placing a [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) directly onto a [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) without ever contacting the [Load Zone](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#loadzone).

Significant Q&As:

- [Q&A 2659](https://www.robotevents.com/VIQRC/2025-2026/QA/2659) \- Match Loads do not have to be placed in vertical positions

##### <R1>

<R1>One Robot per Team. Each [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) can only bring one (1) [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) to a given event. Though it is expected that [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) will make changes to their [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) at the event, a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) is limited to only one (1) [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), and a given [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) may only be used by one (1) [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team). The VEX IQ system is intended to be a mobile robotics design platform. As such, a VEX IQ Robotics Competition [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), for the purposes of the VEX IQ Robotics Competition, has the following subsystems:

- Subsystem 1: Mobile robotic base including wheels, tracks, or any other mechanism that allows the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) to navigate the majority of the flat playing [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) surface. For a stationary [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), the robotic base without wheels would be considered Subsystem 1.
- Subsystem 2: Power and control system that includes a VEX IQ legal battery, a VEX IQ control system, and associated Smart Motors for the mobile robotic base. Also includes the VEX IQ pneumatic air pump and solenoids if used on the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).
- Subsystem 3: Additional mechanisms (and associated Smart Motors) that allow manipulation of [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) or navigation/manipulation of Field Elements.

Given the above definitions, a minimum [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) for use in any VEX IQ Robotics Competition event (including Skills Challenges) must consist of subsystems 1 and 2 above. Thus, if you are swapping out an entire subsystem 1 or 2, you have now created a second [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) and are no longer legal.

1. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may not compete with one [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) while a second is being modified or assembled at a competition.
2. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may not have an assembled second [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) on hand at a competition that is used to repair or swap parts with the first [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).
3. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may not switch back and forth between multiple [Robots](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) during a competition.
