[Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) must remain in the red [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) during [Driving Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#drivingskillsmatch), except when legally interacting with their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) per rule [<GG10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg10).

##### <RSC5>

<RSC5>Handling Robots during an Autonomous Coding Skills Match. A [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may handle their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) as many times as desired during an [Autonomous Coding Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch).

1. Upon handling the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), it must be immediately brought back to a legal starting position.




1. [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) may reset or adjust the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) as desired from this position, including pressing buttons on the Robot Brain or activating sensors.
2. Any [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) being controlled by the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) while being handled must be removed from the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), and can be reintroduced by a Loader in accordance with [<SG6>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#sg6) and [<RSC4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#rsc4). In the context of this rule, “controlled” implies that the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) was manipulating the [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject), and not simply touching it. For example, if the [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) would move with the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) either vertically or while turning, then the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) is “controlling” that [Scoring Object](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject). No other [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) should be moved or adjusted.
3. As described in rule [<S1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#s1), [Students](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#student) cannot step into the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) at any time during a [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). If the [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) cannot reach the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) due to the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) being in the center of the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), they may ask the [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee) to pick up the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) and hand it to the [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) for placement according to the conditions above. The [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) does not get a new [Preload](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#preload) [Pin](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#pin) during this reset.
2. During an [Autonomous Coding Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch), [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) may move freely around the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field), and are not restricted to the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation) when not handling their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot).




1. The rest of [<GG1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg1), which states that [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) are not allowed to use any communication devices during their [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), still applies.
2. An intent of this exception is to permit [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) who wish to “stage” [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) handling during an [Autonomous Coding Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch) to do so without excessive running back and forth to the [Driver Station](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driverstation).

This rule is an explicit exception to rules [<GG4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg4) and the Violation Note for [<GG10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg10), and may be used as part of a [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) strategy for [Autonomous Coding Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch).

[Driving Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#drivingskillsmatch) are still governed by [<GG4>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg4) & the Violation Note for [<GG10>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg10), especially for strategic [Violations](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#violation).

##### <RSC6>

<RSC6>Starting an Autonomous Coding Skills Match. [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) must start a [Robot’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) [Autonomous Coding Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch) routine by pressing a button on the Robot Brain or manually activating a sensor. Because there is no VEX IQ Controller hand-off, only one (1) [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) is required for an [Autonomous Coding Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch) (though [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) may still have two (2) if desired).

1. Pre- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) sensor calibration is considered part of the standard pre- [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) setup time (i.e., the time when the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) would typically be turning on the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot), moving any mechanisms to their desired legal start position, etc.).
2. Pressing a button on the VEX IQ Controller to begin the routine is not permitted. To avoid any confusion, [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) are advised not to bring controllers to [Autonomous Coding Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch).

In accordance with [<GG3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#gg3), [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) should be mindful of event schedules and set their [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) up as promptly as possible. The definition of “prompt” is at the discretion of the [Event Partner](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#eventpartner) and [Head Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#headreferee), and could depend on things like how much time is left for the Skills Challenge [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field)(s) to be open, how many [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) are waiting in line, etc. As a general guideline, three seconds to calibrate a Gyro Sensor would be acceptable, but three minutes to debug a program would not.

##### <RSC7>

<RSC7>Autonomous means “no humans.” During an [Autonomous Coding Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch), [Drive Team Members](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driveteammembers) are not permitted to activate any controls on their VEX IQ Controller, and cannot manually trigger sensors (including the Vision Sensor) in any way, even without touching them.

1. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) cannot use VEX IQ Controllers for any purpose in [Autonomous Coding Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch), and are advised not to bring controllers to the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field). If there is a controller at the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) during an [Autonomous Coding Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#autonomouscodingskillsmatch), it should be placed on the [Floor](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#floor) outside the [Field](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#field) and remain untouched until after the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).

##### <RSC8>

<RSC8>Skills Stop Time. If a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) wishes to end their [Robot Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch) early, they may elect to record a [Skills Stop Time](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#skillsstoptime). This is used as a tiebreaker for [Robot Skills Challenge](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillschallenge) rankings. A [Skills Stop Time](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#skillsstoptime) does not affect a [Team’s](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) score for a given [Robot Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch). [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) and field staff must agree prior to the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) on the signal that will be used to end the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) early.

1. As noted in the definition of [Skills Stop Time](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#skillsstoptime), the moment when the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) ends early is defined as the moment when the [Robot](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robot) and [Scoring Objects](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scoringobject) have come to a rest and the [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) provides the agreed upon visual and audio signal to the [Scorekeeper Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scorekeeperreferee).
2. [Teams](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) who intend to attempt a [Skills Stop Time](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#skillsstoptime) must “opt-in” by verbally confirming with the [Scorekeeper Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scorekeeperreferee) prior to the [Robot Skills Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch). If no notification is given prior to the start of the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match), then the [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) forfeits their option to record a [Skills Stop Time](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#skillsstoptime) for that [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).
3. This conversation should include informing the [Scorekeeper Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scorekeeperreferee) which [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) will signal the stop. The [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) may only be ended early by a [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) for that [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).
4. The agreed-upon signal to stop the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match) must be both verbal and visual, such as [Drivers](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) crossing their arms in an “X” or placing their VEX IQ Controller on the ground.
5. It is recommended that the [Driver](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#driver) also provides a verbal notice that they are approaching their [Skills Stop Time](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#skillsstoptime), such as counting out “3-2-1-stop.”
6. If a [Team](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#team) runs multiple [Robot Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch) in a row, they must reconfirm their [Skills Stop Time](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#skillsstoptime) choice with the [Scorekeeper Referee](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#scorekeeperreferee) prior to each [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match).
7. Any questions regarding a [Skills Stop Time](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#skillsstoptime) should be reviewed and settled immediately following the [Match](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#match). [<T1>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t1) and [<T3>](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#t3) apply to [Robot Skills Matches](https://www.vexrobotics.com/mix-and-match-manual#robotskillsmatch).

"
